**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Chemical Compound                  Process/Source
1. Carbon Dioxide                       Enhanced Weathering
2. Carbonic Acid                         Decomposition of organic matter
3. Methane                               Coal Combustion
4. Carbon Dioxide                       Ambient Air Capture


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 1 and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, and 4 only

**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

Enhanced weathering is a geological process that involves the reaction of silicate rocks with carbon dioxide from the atmosphere, leading to the permanent sequestration of carbon.  Therefore, pair 1 is correctly matched.  Decomposition of organic matter, a biological process, releases carbon dioxide into the atmosphere as a byproduct. This makes pair 2 a correct match.  Ambient Air Capture is a technology designed specifically to remove carbon dioxide directly from the ambient air.  Pair 4 is thus correctly matched.  Coal combustion, however, primarily emits carbon dioxide, not methane (although methane is also a byproduct).  Methane is a greenhouse gas, but its primary source isn't coal combustion exclusively; it's also released from natural gas leaks, agricultural practices, and other sources. Thus, pair 3 is incorrectly matched.  The correct answer is (d) because pairs 1, 2, and 4 accurately link the chemical compound with its associated process or source.


**2. Consider the following pairs:**

   Material/Substance                   Related Process/Characteristic
1. Fossil Fuels                          Releases Carbon Dioxide
2. Shale Gas                             Composed of Carbon Dioxide
3. Carbon Dioxide                       Forms Carbonic Acid
4. Hydrofluorocarbons (HFCs)         Lower global warming potential than Carbon Dioxide


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 and 3 only
(b) 1, 2, and 3 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 1 only

**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

The combustion of fossil fuels is a significant source of atmospheric carbon dioxide emissions. Therefore, pair 1 is correctly matched.  Carbon dioxide readily reacts with water to form carbonic acid. This makes pair 3 a correct match. Shale gas, while containing hydrocarbons, is not primarily composed of carbon dioxide.  Its main components are methane and ethane.  Pair 2 is therefore incorrect.  Hydrofluorocarbons (HFCs) have a significantly higher global warming potential than carbon dioxide, making pair 4 incorrect. The correct option is (a) as only pairs 1 and 3 represent accurate associations.


**3. Consider the following pairs:**

   Geological Feature/Process           Carbon Dioxide Role
1. Continental Carbonate Stores         Transferred Carbon Dioxide
2. Martian Atmosphere                  Composed of Carbon Dioxide
3. Enhanced Weathering                  Removes Carbon Dioxide
4. Algae Assisted Fuel Cells (AFC)      Releases Carbon Dioxide


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1, 2, and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 4 only

**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Continental carbonate stores represent significant reservoirs of carbon that have been transferred from the atmosphere over geological timescales. Pair 1 is correct. The Martian atmosphere is predominantly composed of carbon dioxide. Pair 2 is also correct. Enhanced weathering is a process that removes carbon dioxide from the atmosphere and stores it in rocks. Pair 3 is correct. Algae Assisted Fuel Cells (AFC) capture carbon dioxide, not release it. Thus, pair 4 is incorrect.  The correct answer is (c) because pairs 1, 2, and 3 show accurate relationships between geological features/processes and the role of carbon dioxide.


**4. Consider the following pairs:**

   Carbon Cycle Component                Associated Process
1. Carbon Cycle                          Involves Carbon Dioxide
2.  Decomposition of Organic Matter     Releases Carbon Dioxide
3. Coal Combustion                       Captures Carbon Dioxide
4.  Carbon Capture Technology          Removes Carbon Dioxide


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1, 2, and 4 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 1, 2, 3, and 4
(d) 1 and 4 only

**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

The carbon cycle is a biogeochemical cycle that involves the cycling of carbon through various reservoirs, including the atmosphere, oceans, and biosphere. Carbon dioxide is a central component of this cycle. Therefore, pair 1 is correctly matched. Decomposition of organic matter releases carbon dioxide into the atmosphere.  Pair 2 is correct. Coal combustion is a major source of carbon dioxide emissions, not a process that captures it. Pair 3 is incorrect. Carbon capture technologies are specifically designed to remove carbon dioxide from various sources. Pair 4 is correctly matched. The correct answer is (a) because pairs 1, 2, and 4 accurately describe the relationships between components of the carbon cycle and associated processes.


**5. Consider the following pairs:**

   Greenhouse Gas                         Process/Effect
1. Carbon Dioxide                       Oxidizes to Methane
2. Methane                               Oxidizes to Carbon Dioxide
3. Carbon Dioxide                       Higher global warming potential than HFCs
4.  HFCs                                 Higher global warming potential than Carbon Dioxide


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 2 and 4 only
(b) 1 and 3 only
(c) 1, 2, and 3 only
(d) 2 and 3 only

**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Methane (CH4) oxidizes in the atmosphere to form carbon dioxide (CO2) and water (H2O). Therefore, pair 2 is correctly matched.  Hydrofluorocarbons (HFCs) possess a significantly higher global warming potential compared to carbon dioxide. This makes pair 4 correct. Carbon dioxide does not oxidize to methane; rather, the opposite is true. Pair 1 is incorrect. Carbon dioxide has a lower global warming potential than HFCs. Pair 3 is incorrect.  The correct answer is (a) since only pairs 2 and 4 are correctly matched.

**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Geological Formation                    Geological Epoch
1. Deccan Traps                           :  Miocene
2. Narmada-Tapi alluvial deposits        :  Pliocene
3. East African Rift (EAR)                :  Pleistocene
4. Continental carbonate stores           :  Holocene


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 3 and 4 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (d) None

**Explanation:**

The Deccan Traps volcanic activity primarily occurred during the late Cretaceous to early Paleogene periods, largely preceding the Miocene epoch.  The Narmada-Tapi alluvial deposits primarily formed during the Pleistocene epoch, not the Pliocene. The East African Rift system began developing during the Oligocene to Miocene epochs, not the Pleistocene.  Continental carbonate stores are formed over long geological timescales, with significant contributions across multiple epochs including the Holocene, but their primary formation is not exclusively confined to this period.  Therefore, none of the pairs are correctly matched according to the provided geological timescale.


**2. Consider the following pairs:**

   Chemical Compound                 Process/Feature
1. Carbon Dioxide                     :  Released during decomposition of organic matter
2. Carbonic Acid                       :  Formed from methane oxidation
3. Ethanol                             :  Reduces petrol emission
4.  Hydrofluorocarbons (HFCs)       :   Higher global warming potential than carbon dioxide


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 4 only
(c) 1, 3 and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, 3 and 4


**Correct Answer:** (c) 1, 3 and 4 only

**Explanation:**

Carbon dioxide is indeed released during the decomposition of organic matter as part of the carbon cycle.  Hydrofluorocarbons (HFCs) do possess a significantly higher global warming potential compared to carbon dioxide. Ethanol, when blended with petrol as a biofuel, contributes to reduced emissions compared to using pure petrol. However, carbonic acid is formed from the reaction of carbon dioxide with water, not from methane oxidation. Methane oxidation primarily yields carbon dioxide and water. Therefore, only pairs 1, 3, and 4 are correctly matched.


**3. Consider the following pairs:**

   Biological Molecule                  Function/Characteristic

(b) 1, 2 and 3 only
(c) 1, 2, 3 and 4
(d) 1, 2 and 4 only


**Correct Answer:** (b) 1, 2 and 3 only

**Explanation:**

DNA is the template for transcription, producing messenger RNA (mRNA). RNA, specifically mRNA, is translated into proteins by ribosomes. **7. Consider the following pairs:**

   Isotope                       Type of Uranium
1. 238U                         :   Fissile
2. 235U                         :   Fertile
3. U-234                        :   Fissile
Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

235U is a fissile isotope of uranium, meaning it can sustain a nuclear chain reaction. 238U is a fertile isotope, meaning it can be converted into a fissile isotope (plutonium-239) through neutron capture. U-234 is also a fissile isotope but less abundant than U-235. The question tests understanding of the different isotopes of uranium and their nuclear properties. The distractors use similar numbering to confuse the candidate.

(c) 1, 2, and 3
(d) 2 and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Lead has been historically used in paints and pigments, though regulations have significantly reduced its use.  Lead can be found in some plastic toys, particularly those manufactured in countries with less stringent regulations.  Some traditional Ayurvedic medicines may contain lead as a contaminant or ingredient. The question requires knowledge of the presence of lead in various products and the historical context of its use. The options include both current and historical contexts to test the comprehensive knowledge of the candidate.

**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Chemical Compound                    Property/Effect
1. Sulphur dioxide                       Contributes to ozone depletion
2. Carbon monoxide                       Causes respiratory problems
3. Carbonic acid                         Reacts with limestone to form calcium bicarbonate
4. Ammonia                              Used in fertilizer production
5.  Hydrogen sulfide                    Source of geothermal energy


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 4 only
(c) 3 and 5 only
(d) 2, 3, and 4 only

**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

Option (d) is correct because pairs 2, 3, and 4 represent accurate factual relationships. Carbon monoxide is a well-known air pollutant that causes respiratory problems due to its binding affinity to hemoglobin, reducing oxygen transport in the blood. Carbonic acid, formed by the reaction of carbon dioxide and water, reacts with limestone (calcium carbonate) to produce calcium bicarbonate, a process relevant to cave formation and water hardness. Ammonia is a crucial component in the production of various nitrogen-based fertilizers, playing a vital role in agriculture.

Option (a) is incorrect because sulphur dioxide primarily contributes to acid rain and respiratory issues, not directly to ozone depletion. While it can indirectly influence ozone levels, the primary ozone-depleting substances are chlorofluorocarbons (CFCs) and other halocarbons.

Option (b) is incorrect as it excludes the correct pairing of carbonic acid and its reaction with limestone.  While ammonia is used in fertilizer production, the omission of the accurate relationship between carbonic acid and limestone makes this option incomplete.

Option (c) is incorrect because, while hydrogen sulfide is indeed found in geothermal sources, the inclusion of only this pair and the exclusion of the other correctly matched pairs makes this option faulty.

Therefore, option (d) encompasses all the correctly matched pairs, exhibiting a precise understanding of the chemical properties and applications of the compounds listed.



**2. Consider the following pairs:**

   Process                                    Source/Product
1. Photosynthesis                           Releases carbon dioxide
2.  Combustion of fossil fuels            Produces sulphur dioxide
3.  Electrolysis of water                    Produces hydrogen
4. Steam reforming of hydrocarbons       Produces grey hydrogen
5. Transesterification                     Produces biodiesel


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2, 3, and 4 only
(c) 3, 4, and 5 only
(d) 2, 3, 4, and 5 only

**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Option (c) is correct because the pairs 3, 4, and 5 accurately reflect the processes and their outcomes. Electrolysis of water uses an electric current to split water molecules into hydrogen and oxygen.  Steam reforming of hydrocarbons, a common method for hydrogen production, generates "grey" hydrogen because it releases carbon dioxide. Transesterification is a chemical process that converts vegetable oils or animal fats into biodiesel.

Option (b) is incorrect because photosynthesis releases oxygen, not carbon dioxide.  Photosynthesis consumes carbon dioxide and produces oxygen as a byproduct.

Option (a) is incorrect for the same reason as (b); it incorrectly states that photosynthesis releases carbon dioxide.

Option (d) is incorrect because it includes the incorrect pairing of photosynthesis and carbon dioxide release.

The other options fail to correctly identify the products or byproducts of the given processes, demonstrating a lack of understanding of fundamental chemistry. Option (c) showcases a clear comprehension of the chemical processes involved and their respective products.



**3. Consider the following pairs:**

   Mineral                                    Chemical Element/Use
1. Limestone                                 Contains magnesium
2. Magnesite                                Contains calcium
3. Dolomite                                 Related to magnesite
4. Pyroxene                                 Contains magnesium
5. Olivine                                  Contains calcium


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 3 and 4 only
(c) 2 and 5 only
(d) 1, 2, and 5 only

**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Option (b) is correct because only pairs 3 and 4 are accurately matched.  Dolomite is a carbonate mineral closely related to magnesite, often found in similar geological formations. Pyroxene is a group of silicate minerals that commonly contain magnesium.

Option (a) is incorrect because limestone is primarily composed of calcium carbonate and does not contain significant amounts of magnesium.

Option (c) is incorrect because magnesite is a magnesium carbonate mineral; it does not contain calcium. Similarly, olivine is a silicate mineral rich in magnesium and iron, and it does not contain significant calcium.

Option (d) is incorrect for the reasons stated above concerning limestone, magnesite, and olivine.

The other options demonstrate a misunderstanding of the chemical composition of these minerals. Option (b) shows a precise understanding of the mineralogical relationships and elemental compositions.



**4. With reference to alternative energy sources, consider the following pairs:**

   Energy Source                          Characteristic/Process
1. Biodiesel                               Produced through fermentation
2. Ethanol                                  Produced through transesterification
3. Hydrogen                               Produced via electrolysis of water
4. Methanol                                Used in fuel cells
5. Biofuels                                Carbon-neutral potential


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 3 and 5 only
(c) 2 and 4 only
(d) 3, 4, and 5 only

**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Option (b) is correct. Hydrogen is indeed produced via the electrolysis of water, a process that splits water molecules into hydrogen and oxygen using electricity.  Biofuels, derived from biological sources, have the potential to be carbon-neutral if the carbon dioxide released during combustion is offset by the carbon dioxide absorbed during the growth of the biomass.

Option (a) is incorrect because biodiesel is produced through transesterification, not fermentation. Fermentation is used in the production of ethanol.

Option (c) is incorrect because ethanol is produced through fermentation, and while methanol can be a fuel, its primary use is not in fuel cells; hydrogen is more commonly used in fuel cells.

Option (d) is incorrect because it includes the incorrect pairings of biodiesel and fermentation, and ethanol and transesterification.

The other options demonstrate a lack of understanding of biofuel production methods and applications. Option (b) highlights a precise understanding of the processes involved in hydrogen production and the potential of biofuels.


**5. With reference to the chemical compounds and their properties, consider the following pairs:**

   Compound                                 Property/Use
1.  Ethylene                                Used in artificial ripening of fruits
2. Liquid nitrogen                         Used in cryotherapy
3.  Methanol                                Toxic if ingested
4.  Ammonia                                Used as a refrigerant
5.  Sulphuric acid                         Used in the production of fertilizers


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 3, 4, and 5 only
(c) 1, 2, and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, 3, and 5 only

**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

Option (d) is the correct answer because all pairs 1, 2, 3, and 5 accurately reflect the properties and uses of the listed compounds. Ethylene gas is used to artificially ripen fruits, liquid nitrogen's extremely low temperature makes it suitable for cryotherapy, methanol is highly toxic if ingested, and sulphuric acid is a crucial component in the production of various fertilizers.

Option (a) is incorrect because it excludes the accurate pairings of methanol and its toxicity and sulphuric acid and its use in fertilizer production.

Option (b) is incorrect as it incorrectly states that ammonia is used as a refrigerant (while it has been used historically, it's not a common modern application due to safety concerns).

Option (c) is incorrect because it excludes the accurate pairing of sulphuric acid and its use in fertilizer production.

The other options contain one or more inaccurate pairings, showcasing a lack of thorough understanding of the chemical properties and applications of these substances.  Option (d) displays a complete and accurate understanding of the facts.

**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Fuel Type                     Characteristic/Use
1. Diesel                         Used in heavy-duty engines
2. Petrol                          Has an energy density of 40-44 MJ/kg
3. Kerosene                      Adulterant of gasoline and diesel
4. Biodiesel                      Alternative to diesel
5. Methanol                       Alternative fuel for both petrol and diesel

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1, 2, and 3 only
(b) 1, 2, 4, and 5 only
(c) 1, 3, 4, and 5 only
(d) All of the above


**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

All the pairs are correctly matched based on established facts and common knowledge about fuel types.  Diesel is predominantly used in heavy-duty engines due to its higher energy density and suitability for such applications. Petrol, with its energy density ranging from 40 to 44 MJ/kg, is a common fuel for internal combustion engines. Kerosene, while having its own uses, is unfortunately often used as an adulterant in gasoline and diesel fuel, reducing their quality and impacting engine performance. Biodiesel serves as a renewable and sustainable alternative to conventional diesel fuel, reducing reliance on fossil fuels. Finally, methanol (CH3OH), also known as wood alcohol, is a colorless and fairly volatile liquid, considered an alternative fuel source for both petrol and diesel engines, although its widespread adoption faces challenges related to toxicity and infrastructure.  Therefore, all five pairs represent accurate relationships between the fuel type and its characteristic or use.



**2. Consider the following pairs:**

   Chemical Compound              Reaction/Product
1. Carbonic acid                  Reacts with limestone to form calcium carbonate
2. Carbon dioxide                  Forms carbonic acid in water
3. Calcium bicarbonate            Produced by the reaction of carbonic acid and limestone
4. CO2                             Reacts to form Calcium Bicarbonate
5. Methanol                        Alternative fuel for diesel


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 1, 2, and 3 only
(c) 2 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, 3, and 4 only


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Carbonic acid (HCO) reacts with limestone (calcium carbonate, CaCO) to form calcium bicarbonate (Ca(HCO)), a soluble compound. This reaction is crucial in the formation of caves. Carbon dioxide (CO) dissolving in water forms carbonic acid, a weak acid.  Calcium bicarbonate is indeed a product of the reaction between carbonic acid and limestone. However, CO2 alone cannot directly react to form calcium bicarbonate; it needs to first form carbonic acid in water. Methanol is an alternative fuel but its relation is not directly with this chemical reaction. Therefore, options (a), (c), and (d) are incomplete representations of the accurate chemical reactions and products.  Only option (b) accurately reflects the correct pairings.



**3. Consider the following pairs:**

   Crop                     Characteristic/Requirement
1. Sugarcane                 Requires significant water usage
2. Sugarcane                 Grown in temperate regions
3. Sugarcane                 Produced in North Bengal
4. Sugarcane                 Economic alternative to sugar imports
5.  Mustard                   Contains high levels of glucosinolates


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1, 3, and 4 only
(b) 1 and 4 only
(c) 1, 3, 4, and 5 only
(d) 1, 4, and 5 only


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Sugarcane cultivation is indeed water-intensive, requiring substantial irrigation. North Bengal is a significant sugarcane-producing region in India.  Domestic sugarcane production serves as an important alternative to relying on sugar imports.  However, sugarcane is a tropical and subtropical crop; it does not thrive in temperate regions.  While mustard does contain glucosinolates, the question focuses on sugarcane characteristics. Therefore, options (b), (c), and (d) are incorrect because they include the incorrect statement about sugarcane's suitability for temperate regions. Option (a) correctly identifies the accurate pairings related to sugarcane's cultivation and economic significance.


**4. Consider the following pairs:**

   Biomolecule                 Component/Application
1. Proteins                     Composed of amino acids
2. Proteins                     Essential for synthesis of iron (Fe) in plants
3. Amino acids                  Building block of proteins
4.  Ethanol                      Derived from sugarcane
5.  Methanol                      Used in synthetic dyestuffs


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1, 3, and 4 only
(b) 1, 3, and 5 only
(c) 1, 2, 3, and 4 only
(d) All of the above


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Proteins are indeed composed of amino acids linked together in a specific sequence. Amino acids are the fundamental building blocks of proteins. Ethanol is a biofuel derived from the fermentation of sugarcane. Methanol is used in various industrial applications, including the production of synthetic dyestuffs.  However, the statement that proteins are essential for the synthesis of iron in plants is not entirely accurate. While iron is crucial for plant growth and chlorophyll production and plants need proteins for various metabolic processes,  it's not directly involved in *synthesizing* iron itself. Iron is absorbed from the soil. Thus, options (a), (c), and (d) are incorrect due to the inclusion of the inaccurate statement regarding iron synthesis in plants. Only option (b) accurately reflects the correct pairings.


**5. Consider the following pairs:**

   Pollutant/Additive           Fuel Type
1. Lead                           Diesel
2. Tetraethyl lead (TEL)       Petrol
3. Methanol                       Petrol (as an alternative fuel)
4. Lead                           Petrol
5.  Methanol                       Diesel (as an alternative fuel)

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1, 2, and 3 only
(b) 2, 3, and 4 only
(c) 2, 3, and 5 only
(d) 2, 4, and 5 only


**Correct Answer:** (d)


**Explanation:**

Tetraethyl lead (TEL) was historically used as an additive in petrol to improve its octane rating, although its use has largely been phased out due to its environmental toxicity. Methanol is considered an alternative fuel source for both petrol and diesel engines. Lead was indeed historically present as a contaminant in petrol but is not currently a deliberate additive. While methanol is being explored as an alternative fuel for diesel, lead is not a common contaminant in diesel. Therefore, options (a), (b), and (c) contain incorrect pairings.  Only option (d) accurately reflects the presence of TEL in petrol and the exploration of methanol as an alternative fuel for both petrol and diesel.

**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Chemical Compound             Energy Source/Application
1. Methane                         :   Compressed Bio-Gas (CBG)
2. Carbon Dioxide                 :   Heating
3. Ammonia                         :   Electricity Production
4. Sulphuric Acid                  :   Vehicle Fuel

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 2 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b) 1 and 2 only

**Explanation:**

Methane is a major component of biogas, and CBG is a refined form of biogas, making pair 1 correct.  Biogas, primarily composed of methane, is used for heating, making pair 2 correct.  While biogas can be used for electricity production, ammonia itself is not directly an energy source or application derived from biogas.  Sulphuric acid is not directly related to biogas applications; biogas can be used as vehicle fuel (biomethane), but not sulphuric acid. Therefore, only pairs 1 and 2 are correctly matched.  The options are designed to be plausible distractors, testing the candidate's precise knowledge of biogas composition and applications.


**2. With reference to Biogas production, consider the following pairs:**

   Biological Process             Energy Source
1. Anaerobic digestion            :   Compressed Biogas (CBG)
2. Anaerobic decomposition of biomass :  Biogas
3.  Aerobic decomposition of organic matter : Methane
4. Microbial Inoculums           :  Biogas


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 2 and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, and 4 only


**Correct Answer:** (c) 2 and 4 only

**Explanation:**

Biogas is produced through the anaerobic decomposition of biomass, making pair 2 correct.  Anaerobic Microbial Inoculums are used to enhance biogas production, hence pair 4 is also correct.  While anaerobic digestion is a key process in biogas production, CBG is a refined form of biogas, not directly produced by anaerobic digestion alone. Aerobic decomposition does not produce methane; it's anaerobic decomposition that yields methane.  The incorrect pairings act as effective distractors, testing the candidate's understanding of the nuances of biogas production processes.



**3. Consider the following pairs:**

   Chemical Element          Application/Occurrence
1. Sulphur                      :   Constituent of Biodiesel
2. Iron                          :  Component of Haematite
3. Zinc                          :   Used in Rubber Industry
4. Manganese                    :   Deoxidizes Sulphur


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 3 and 4 only
(d) 2, 3, and 4 only


**Correct Answer:** (d) 2, 3, and 4 only

**Explanation:**

Iron is a major component of the iron ore haematite, making pair 2 correct. Zinc finds extensive use in the rubber industry, making pair 3 correct. Manganese is used as a deoxidizer for sulphur, which is crucial in various industrial processes, making pair 4 correct. Biodiesel has a low sulphur content; sulphur is not a constituent. The incorrect pairing serves as a distractor, highlighting the need for precise knowledge of industrial applications and mineral composition.



**4. With reference to the impact of Temperature, consider the following pairs:**

  Environmental Factor/Process       Effect of Temperature
1. Anaerobic digestion               :   Optimum temperature range
2.  Water holding capacity of air     : Increases with temperature
3.  Soil formation                  :   Influences rate
4.  Coral bleaching                  :   Caused by high temperatures


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1, 2, and 3 only
(c) 2 and 3 only
(d) 1, 3, and 4 only


**Correct Answer:** (d) 1, 3, and 4 only

**Explanation:**

Anaerobic digestion has an optimum temperature range for efficient microbial activity. Soil formation is significantly influenced by temperature, affecting various chemical and biological processes.  Coral bleaching is primarily caused by elevated water temperatures. The water holding capacity of air decreases with increasing temperature due to increased molecular kinetic energy. The inclusion of the incorrect statement about water holding capacity acts as a strong distractor, ensuring the question tests a nuanced understanding of the topic.


**5. Consider the following pairs:**

    Chemical Compound             Source/Application
1. Nitrate                         :   Absorbed by plants

4. Carbon Dioxide                  :   Byproduct of Anaerobic Digestion


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1, 2, and 3 only
(c) 2, 3, and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, 3, and 4


**Correct Answer:** (d) 1, 2, 3, and 4

**Explanation:**

Plants absorb nitrates as a primary source of nitrogen. Ammonia is a crucial raw material for urea production in the fertilizer industry. Methane is a significant component of biogas. Carbon dioxide is produced as a byproduct during anaerobic digestion. All four pairs accurately reflect the source and application of these chemical compounds. **1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Commodity                     Associated Chemical Compound
1.  Potato                         Solanine
2.  Onion                          Allyl propyl disulfide
3.  Tomato                         Lycopene
4.  Polyethylene                 Ethylene

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 2 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (d) 1, 2, and 3 only

**Explanation:**

Solanine is a glycoalkaloid found in potatoes, particularly in the sprouts and green parts.  High levels of solanine can be toxic. Allyl propyl disulfide is a sulfur-containing compound responsible for the characteristic pungent odor and flavor of onions. Lycopene is a carotenoid pigment that gives tomatoes their red color and is also a potent antioxidant.  Polyethylene is a polymer, but it's not directly associated with these vegetables in the same way as the other compounds. While ethylene is used in the artificial ripening of tomatoes, it's not a constituent compound of the tomato itself.  Therefore, only pairs 1, 2, and 3 represent accurate associations between a commodity and a chemical compound naturally present within or closely associated with its production.


**2. Consider the following pairs:**

   Fusion Technology              Associated Research Facility
1.  Tokamak                         ITER
2.  Magnetic Confinement Fusion  JET
3.  Tokamak                         EAST
4.  Tokamak                         JT-60

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 3 only
(c) 1, 3, and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, 3, and 4


**Correct Answer:** (c) 1, 3, and 4 only

**Explanation:**

The ITER project is a large-scale international collaboration focused on developing a tokamak-based fusion reactor.  EAST (Experimental Advanced Superconducting Tokamak) and JT-60 are both tokamak-type fusion experimental reactors.  While JET (Joint European Torus) is also a tokamak, the pair linking magnetic confinement fusion to JET is inaccurate because while JET utilizes magnetic confinement, it's not solely defined by that technology; it's a specific example of a tokamak which is a type of magnetic confinement fusion device.  Therefore, options 1, 3, and 4 correctly link a fusion technology (Tokamak) with an associated research facility.  Option 2 incorrectly generalizes a type of fusion to a specific research facility.


**3. Consider the following pairs:**

   Plant Hormone                   Primary Function
1.  Auxin                            Apical Dominance
2.  Gibberellin                      Cell Division
3.  Cytokinin                         Cell Elongation
4.  Abscisic Acid                   Growth Inhibition


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 4 only
(c) 1, 2, and 4 only
(d) 1, 3, and 4 only


**Correct Answer:** (b) 1 and 4 only

**Explanation:**

Auxins are plant hormones primarily responsible for apical dominance, the phenomenon where the main stem grows more vigorously than lateral branches. Abscisic acid (ABA) is a plant hormone that inhibits growth, often in response to stress conditions. While gibberellins are involved in cell elongation and cytokinins play a role in cell division, the primary functions are not solely confined to these aspects; they also influence other aspects of plant growth and development.  Hence only the pairs related to auxin and abscisic acid accurately reflect the primary functions of these plant hormones.

**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Celestial Body          Phenomenon Influenced
1. Moon                     :    Earth's Rotation
2. Sun                       :    Lunar Tides
3. Earth                     :    Solar Flares
4. Jupiter                   :    Neap Tides

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 3 only
(c) 3 and 4 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

The Moon's gravitational pull significantly influences Earth's rotation, causing tidal bulges and slowing down the Earth's spin over geological time.  This tidal interaction is a well-established phenomenon in celestial mechanics. Option 2 is incorrect because lunar tides are primarily influenced by the Moon's gravity, not the Sun's. While the Sun does exert a tidal force, the Moon's proximity to Earth makes its effect dominant. Option 3 is incorrect; solar flares are powerful bursts of radiation from the Sun, unrelated to Earth's rotation or the Moon's influence. Option 4 is incorrect as Neap tides are caused by the combined gravitational pull of the Sun and Moon when they are at right angles to each other, minimizing the tidal range.  Therefore, only the pairing of the Moon and its influence on Earth's rotation is accurately matched.


**2. With reference to the Earth's atmosphere, consider the following pairs:**

   Atmospheric Component     Source
1. Carbon Dioxide (CO2)     :     Volcanic Eruptions
2. Oxygen (O2)              :     Photosynthesis
3. Nitrogen (N2)            :     Fossil Fuels
4. Methane (CH4)           :     Decomposition of Organic Matter

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 and 4 only
(c) 1, 2, and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, 3, and 4


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Volcanic eruptions are a significant natural source of carbon dioxide, releasing it into the atmosphere. Photosynthesis, the process by which plants convert light energy into chemical energy, is the primary source of atmospheric oxygen.  Decomposition of organic matter, including plant and animal remains, produces methane as a byproduct.  While nitrogen is abundant in the atmosphere, fossil fuels are not a primary source of atmospheric nitrogen; they are primarily composed of carbon and hydrogen.  Instead, the majority of atmospheric nitrogen originates from geological processes. Thus, pairs 1, 2, and 4 are correctly matched.


**3. Consider the following pairs:**

   Metal                     Use in Industry
1. Copper                    :     Rubber Industry
2. Zinc                      :     Electrical Industry
3. Aluminium                 :     Construction Industry
4. Iron                       :     Aerospace Industry


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 3 and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, 3, and 4


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Aluminium is extensively used in the construction industry due to its lightweight yet strong properties. Iron and its alloys (steel) are critical materials in aerospace engineering for their strength-to-weight ratio and ability to withstand high stresses. Copper is primarily used in the electrical industry due to its excellent conductivity. Zinc finds considerable application in corrosion protection (galvanization) of steel and iron. The rubber industry does not heavily rely on copper as a primary component. Therefore, only the pairs relating to aluminium's use in construction and iron's role in aerospace are correctly matched.


**4. With reference to minerals and their primary uses, consider the following pairs:**

   Mineral                     Primary Use
1. Bauxite                     :     Production of Iron
2. Magnetite                 :     Production of Aluminium
3. Sphalerite                  :     Production of Zinc
4. Hematite                   :     Production of Copper

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 3 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 2 and 4 only


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Sphalerite is the primary ore of zinc, from which zinc metal is extracted. Bauxite is the principal ore of aluminum, not iron. Magnetite is a crucial iron ore, not an aluminum ore. Hematite is also a significant iron ore, not a copper ore.  Therefore, only the pairing of sphalerite with its use in zinc production is correct.


**5. Consider the following pairs:**

   Chemical Element       Abundance in Earth's Crust

(b) 3 and 4 only
(c) 2, 3, and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, 3, and 4

**Explanation:**

Oxygen is the most abundant element in the Earth's crust, followed by silicon and then aluminum. Iron is a significant component but not the third most abundant, ranking lower than aluminum. Therefore, only the pairings of silicon as the second most abundant and aluminum as the most abundant are correct.

    Gas                     Percentage Composition (Approximate)

**7. Consider the following pairs:**

   Chemical Compound         Use

Potassium nitrate is historically used in photography as an oxidizer in some processes. Sodium chloride (common salt) is used for food preservation due to its antimicrobial properties. **8. Consider the following pairs:**

   Vitamin                     Deficiency Disease
1. Niacin                     :    Rickets

3. Vitamin D                  :    Pellagra
4. Vitamin K                  :    Night Blindness

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 2 and 4 only


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Thiamine deficiency leads to beriberi.  Niacin deficiency causes pellagra, not rickets. Vitamin D deficiency results in rickets. Vitamin K deficiency does not cause night blindness; that is usually associated with vitamin A deficiency.  Therefore, only the pairing of thiamine with beriberi is correctly matched.

**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Radiation Type                     Medical Application
1. X-rays                              :   Radiation therapy for cancer
2. Gamma rays                          :   Diagnostic imaging of bones
3. Ultrasound waves                   :   Fetal growth monitoring

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2 and 3


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

X-rays are indeed used in radiation therapy to target and destroy cancerous cells.  This is a well-established and widely used medical application.  Option (a) is therefore correct.

Option (b) is incorrect because while gamma rays are used in some medical applications,  they are not primarily used for diagnostic imaging of bones; X-rays are far more common for this purpose.  Gamma rays are more often used in radiation therapy, similar to X-rays, but with different penetration capabilities.

Option (c) is incorrect because, although ultrasound waves are used for fetal growth monitoring, this does not make the pairing of gamma rays with bone imaging correct. The correct pairing of ultrasound waves with fetal growth monitoring is overshadowed by the incorrect pairing of gamma rays with bone imaging.

Option (d) is incorrect because it combines the correct pairing of X-rays with radiation therapy with two incorrect pairings.


**2. Consider the following pairs:**

   Mineral                                  Metal
1. Ilmenite                               :   Titanium
2. Bauxite                                 :   Aluminum
3. Hematite                               :   Iron

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2 and 3


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Ilmenite is a titanium-iron oxide mineral, making the first pair correct. Bauxite is the principal ore of aluminum, making the second pair correct.  Therefore, option (b) is the correct answer.

Option (a) is incorrect as it excludes the correctly matched pair of Bauxite and Aluminum.

Option (c) is incorrect as it incorrectly includes Hematite as a source of Titanium; Hematite is primarily an iron ore.

Option (d) is incorrect because it includes the incorrect pairing of Hematite with Iron. While Hematite is an important iron ore, the question focuses on precise and accurate pairings, and the inclusion of the inaccurate pairing makes the entire option incorrect.



**3. Consider the following pairs:**

   Atomic Property                         Description
1. Atomic Number                         :   Number of neutrons in an atom
2. Mass Number                           :   Sum of protons and electrons
3. Isotopes                               :   Atoms of the same element with different numbers of neutrons

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) 1, 2 and 3


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

The atomic number is defined as the number of protons in an atom's nucleus, not neutrons.  The mass number is the sum of protons and neutrons, not protons and electrons.  Isotopes are atoms of the same element with the same number of protons but a different number of neutrons.  Only the third pair is correctly matched. Therefore, (c) is correct.

Option (a) is incorrect because the description of atomic number is wrong.

Option (b) is incorrect because the description of mass number is wrong.

Option (d) is incorrect because it includes two incorrect pairings.

   Material                                 Use in Production

Option (a) is incorrect as it omits the correct pairing of graphite and pencil lead.

Option (c) is incorrect as it includes the incorrect pairing of ilmenite with gallium.

Option (d) is incorrect as it includes the incorrect pairing of ilmenite with gallium.


**5. Consider the following pairs:**

   Physical Phenomenon                     Example

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) Only one
(b) Only two
(c) All three
(d) None

X-rays are a type of ionizing radiation, and are used extensively in medical imaging.  The photoacoustic effect describes the generation of ultrasound waves from the absorption of light, a phenomenon used in certain medical imaging techniques. Option (c) is incorrect because one pair is incorrectly matched.

Option (d) is incorrect because two pairs are correctly matched.

Here are some UPSC-style multiple-choice questions based on the provided text, adhering to all specified criteria.  Each question includes a correct answer and a detailed explanation.


**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Chemical Compound             Application/Property
1. Ethylene (CH)                 :   Used in cryotherapy
2. Liquid Nitrogen (N)            :   Artificial ripening of fruits
3. Methanol (CHOH)              :   Component in some hand sanitizers
4. Fomepizole                      :   Antidote for methanol poisoning


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 3 and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Option (c) is correct because only pairs 3 and 4 are correctly matched. Methanol (CHOH), also known as wood alcohol, is a component found in some hand sanitizers, as noted in the text's discussion of the US recall of hand sanitizers containing methanol.  Fomepizole is explicitly identified as an antidote for methanol poisoning.

Pair 1 is incorrect. Ethylene is used for artificial ripening, not liquid nitrogen.  Liquid nitrogen is used in cryotherapy (freezing) and food transportation. Pair 2 is also incorrect.  The text specifies that ethylene, not liquid nitrogen, is used for artificial ripening of fruits, although its use is regulated. Pair 1 incorrectly swaps the applications of ethylene and liquid nitrogen.


**2. With reference to Glycemic Index (GI) and its implications, consider the following pairs:**

   Food Characteristic/Factor          Effect/Relationship
1. High GI foods                       :   Slow digestion, sustained blood sugar levels
2. Amylose                             :   Internal factor affecting GI
3. Glycemic Load (GL)                 :   Calculated by subtracting GI from total carbohydrates
4. Prof. David Jenkins                 :   Proposed the Glycemic Load (GL)


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 2 and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Option (b) is correct because only pair 2 is correctly matched. Amylose is correctly identified as an internal factor that influences the Glycemic Index (GI) of food.

Pair 1 is incorrect. High GI foods cause *rapid*, not slow, fluctuations in blood sugar levels.  Pair 3 is incorrect.  Glycemic Load (GL) is calculated by *multiplying*, not subtracting, the GI by the amount of carbohydrates in a serving. Pair 4 is incorrect.  Prof. David Jenkins proposed the Glycemic Index (GI), not the Glycemic Load (GL).


**3. With reference to Avian Influenza (Bird Flu), consider the following pairs:**

   Virus Protein/Characteristic         Effect/Classification
1. Hemagglutinin (H) and Neuraminidase (N) :   Determine LPAI and HPAI virus subtypes
2. LPAI viruses                        :   Cause severe disease and high mortality in poultry
3. HPAI viruses                        :   Cause mild or no disease in poultry
4. World Organisation for Animal Health (WOAH) :  Conducts global influenza surveillance


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Option (a) is correct. Only pair 1 is correctly matched.  The hemagglutinin (H) and neuraminidase (N) proteins on the surface of influenza A viruses are indeed used to classify subtypes.

Pair 2 is incorrect. LPAI viruses cause mild or no disease, not severe disease and high mortality.  Pair 3 is incorrect. HPAI viruses cause severe disease and high mortality, not mild or no disease. Pair 4 is incorrect. The World Organisation for Animal Health (WOAH) collaborates on animal health, but global influenza surveillance is conducted through the WHO's Global Influenza Surveillance and Response System (GISRS).


**4. Consider the following pairs:**

   Medical Technology/Condition       Characteristic/Application
1. Magnetic Resonance Imaging (MRI)    :   Uses ionizing radiation
2. Meningococcal ACWY Vaccine         :   Protects against five strains of meningococcus bacteria
3. Men5CV vaccine                     :   Available in India
4. Thrombosis with Thrombocytopenia Syndrome (TTS) :   Characterized by low platelet count and blood clots


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 4 only
(c) 3 and 4 only
(d) 4 only


**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

Option (d) is correct.  Only pair 4 is correctly matched. Thrombosis with Thrombocytopenia Syndrome (TTS) is accurately described as a condition involving blood clots and low platelet count.

Pair 1 is incorrect. MRI does *not* use ionizing radiation; it uses magnets and radio waves. Pair 2 is incorrect.  The Men5CV vaccine protects against five strains, but the text mentions that the Meningococcal ACWY Vaccine is available in India, not the Men5CV vaccine. Pair 3 is also incorrect for the same reason as pair 2; it mismatches the vaccine availability.


**5. With reference to recent scientific advancements, consider the following pairs:**

   Scientific Concept/Technology      Description/Application
1. Retrotransposons                 :   Genetic elements replicating via reverse transcription
2.  Glucagon-like peptide 1 (GLP-1)  :    A gut hormone that increases blood sugar levels
3.  Weight-loss drugs                 :   Mimic the action of GLP-1 to increase appetite
4.  Covishield vaccine                :   Has never been admitted to have rare side effects


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 1 and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3 only


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Only pair 1 is correctly matched. Retrotransposons are accurately defined as genetic elements that replicate through reverse transcription.

Pair 2 is incorrect. GLP-1 *reduces*, not increases, blood sugar levels by increasing insulin production and decreasing glucagon production. Pair 3 is incorrect. Weight-loss drugs mimic GLP-1 to *suppress* appetite, not increase it. Pair 4 is incorrect.  The text explicitly states that AstraZeneca (the manufacturer of Covishield) admitted to rare side effects, including TTS.

Here are some UPSC-style multiple choice questions based on the provided target content, adhering to all specified criteria.  Each question is designed to be challenging and requires a deep understanding of the facts.


**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Chemical Compound          Associated Process/Effect
1. Formaldehyde                Ozone layer depletion
2. Methane                      Enhanced Greenhouse Effect
3. Carbon Dioxide              Ocean Acidification

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 2 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Option (c) is correct because methane (CH4) and carbon dioxide (CO2) are both potent greenhouse gases, significantly contributing to the enhanced greenhouse effect and subsequent global warming.  Carbon dioxide dissolves in seawater to form carbonic acid, leading to ocean acidification.  Formaldehyde, while a pollutant, does not directly deplete the ozone layer; ozone depletion is primarily associated with chlorofluorocarbons (CFCs) and other ozone-depleting substances.  Therefore, only pairs 2 and 3 are correctly matched.


**2. Consider the following pairs:**

   Biological Entity           Associated Product/Process
1.  Penicillium fungus          Production of Aspirin
2.  Methanogenic archaea       Methane emission
3.  Host cell                   Viral replication


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Option (b) is correct because methanogenic archaea are microorganisms that produce methane through anaerobic respiration, and viruses replicate by invading and utilizing host cells.  Penicillin is produced by *Penicillium* fungi, not *aspirin*. Aspirin is a synthetic compound. Therefore, only pairs 2 and 3 show accurate associations.


**3. With reference to Global Warming, consider the following pairs:**

   Phenomenon/Impact          Causal Factor/Process
1. Increased frequency of heatwaves :   Decreased dissolved oxygen in water
2.  Sea level rise                 :   Thermal expansion of water and melting glaciers
3.  Arctic Amplification           :   Higher absorption of solar radiation at higher latitudes

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 2 only


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Option (b) is correct. Global warming leads to sea level rise due to thermal expansion of water (water expands as it warms) and the melting of glaciers and ice sheets.  Arctic amplification, the phenomenon where the Arctic warms at a faster rate than the global average, is caused by the higher absorption of solar radiation at higher latitudes due to ice-albedo feedback.  While decreased dissolved oxygen in water is a consequence of global warming, its not the direct cause of increased heatwaves; heatwaves are primarily a direct result of rising air temperatures.  Therefore, pairs 2 and 3 are correctly matched.


**4. Consider the following pairs:**

   Gas                                      Impact/Source
1.  Butane                                   Component of LPG
2.  Methane                                 Produced by methanogens
3.  Carbon Dioxide                           Primary product of photosynthesis

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (a)

**Explanation:**

Option (a) is correct. Butane is a major component of liquefied petroleum gas (LPG). Methane is produced by methanogenic archaea and other biological sources. However, the primary product of photosynthesis is glucose, not carbon dioxide;  photosynthesis *consumes* carbon dioxide. Therefore, only pairs 1 and 2 are correctly matched.


**5. Consider the following pairs:**

   Microorganism              Disease/Process
1.  Bacteria                     Viral Replication
2.  Fungi                        Penicillin Production
3.  Viruses                      Invading Host Cells

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) Only one
(b) Only two
(c) All three
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Option (b) is correct. Fungi, specifically *Penicillium* species, are known for producing penicillin. Viruses replicate by invading and taking over host cells. However, bacteria are not directly involved in viral replication; they are separate types of microorganisms. Therefore, only two pairs are correctly matched.


**6. With reference to the effects of Global Warming, consider the following pairs:**

   Effect                                    Mechanism
1. Increased melting of cryosphere       Enhanced greenhouse effect trapping heat
2. Increased incidence of El Nio          Changes in ocean currents and atmospheric pressure
3.  Ocean acidification                     Increased carbon dioxide absorption by oceans

Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?

(a) 1 and 2 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3


**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

All three pairs are correctly matched.  The enhanced greenhouse effect, caused by increased greenhouse gas concentrations due to human activities, traps more heat, leading to increased melting of the cryosphere (ice caps, glaciers, and permafrost).  Changes in ocean currents and atmospheric pressure patterns, influenced by global warming, contribute to the increased frequency and intensity of El Nio events.  Finally, the increased absorption of carbon dioxide by the oceans leads to the formation of carbonic acid, causing ocean acidification.  Therefore, all three pairs accurately describe causal relationships related to global warming.


These questions test factual recall, analysis (identifying correct relationships), and evaluation (determining the accuracy of the pairings).  The distractors are carefully chosen to be plausible but ultimately incorrect, thereby increasing the difficulty level.

**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Type of Malicious Software          Specific Example
1.  Adware                              :   Spyware
2.  Ransomware                          :   Trojan Horse
3.  Rootkit                              :   Keylogger
4.  Virus                                :   Worm


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 3 and 4 only
(d) None


**Correct Answer:** (d) None

**Explanation:**

The question tests the understanding of various types of malicious software and their examples.  Let's analyze each pair:

1. **Adware and Spyware:** While both are unwanted software, they are distinct. Adware displays unwanted advertisements, whereas spyware secretly monitors user activity.  Therefore, this pairing is incorrect.

2. **Ransomware and Trojan Horse:** Ransomware encrypts a user's files and demands a ransom for their release. A Trojan horse disguises itself as legitimate software to gain access to a system.  Although both are malicious, they operate differently; hence, this pairing is incorrect.

3. **Rootkit and Keylogger:** A rootkit provides unauthorized access and control over a computer system, often concealing its presence. A keylogger records keystrokes, which *can* be a component of a rootkit but is not exclusively defined as one. Thus, the pairing is incorrect.

4. **Virus and Worm:** Viruses require a host program to replicate, while worms can self-replicate and spread independently across networks. This pairing is also incorrect.

All pairs present incorrect pairings of malicious software types and their examples.  Therefore, the correct answer is (d) None.  Understanding the nuanced differences between these types of malware is crucial for cybersecurity awareness.


**2. Consider the following pairs:**

   Software Category                     Specific Software
1.  Operating System                    :   Spyware
2.  Application Software                :   Microsoft Word
3.  System Utility Software             :   Disk Defragmenter
4.  Malicious Software                  :   Virus


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 3 and 4 only
(d) 2, 3 and 4 only


**Correct Answer:** (d) 2, 3 and 4 only

**Explanation:**

This question assesses knowledge of software categories and examples. Let's evaluate each pair:

1. **Operating System and Spyware:** An operating system (OS) manages computer hardware and software resources. Spyware is a type of malicious software, not an OS.  Therefore, this pairing is incorrect.

2. **Application Software and Microsoft Word:** Application software performs specific tasks for users, and Microsoft Word is a prime example of word-processing application software. This is a correct pairing.

3. **System Utility Software and Disk Defragmenter:** System utilities manage and maintain computer systems. Disk defragmenter reorganizes fragmented files on a hard drive, a typical system utility function. This is a correct pairing.

4. **Malicious Software and Virus:** Viruses are a type of malicious software designed to damage or disrupt computer systems. This is a correct pairing.

Therefore, only pairs 2, 3, and 4 are correctly matched. The correct answer is (d).  The question tests the ability to classify different software types and recognize their functionalities.


**3. Consider the following pairs:**

   Characteristic of Spyware        Description
1.  Data Theft                       :   Collecting user's Personally Identifiable Information (PII)
2.  System Slowdown                  :   Increased CPU usage due to background processes
3.  Identity Theft                    :   Using stolen data for fraudulent activities
4.  Network compromise              :   Installing backdoors for remote access


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1, 2 and 3 only
(c) 1, 2, 3 and 4 only
(d) 2 and 4 only


**Correct Answer:** (c) 1, 2, 3 and 4 only

**Explanation:**

This question delves into the characteristics and effects of spyware.

1. **Data theft and PII collection:** Spyware's primary function is often stealing sensitive data, including Personally Identifiable Information (PII). This is a correct match.

2. **System slowdown and increased CPU usage:** Spyware running in the background consumes system resources, leading to performance degradation.  This is correctly matched.

3. **Identity theft and fraudulent activities:** Stolen PII from spyware can be used for identity theft and various fraudulent activities. This is a correct match.

4. **Network compromise and backdoors:** Advanced spyware can create backdoors, enabling remote access and control, thus compromising the network security. This is a correct match.

All four pairs accurately describe characteristics and effects of spyware.  Therefore, the correct option is (c). The question assesses the understanding of spyware's impact on user systems and data security.


**4. Consider the following pairs:**

   Category of Malware              Method of Operation
1.  Trojan Horse                     :   Disguised as legitimate software
2.  Spyware                           :   Monitors user activity secretly
3.  Ransomware                        :   Encrypts files and demands ransom
4.  Virus                             :   Self-replicates and spreads rapidly


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 1, 2, and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, 3, and 4


**Correct Answer:** (d) 1, 2, 3, and 4

**Explanation:**

This question tests the knowledge of different malware categories and their operational methods.

1. **Trojan Horse and disguise:** Trojan horses are malicious programs disguised as legitimate software to trick users into installing them. This is correctly matched.

2. **Spyware and secret monitoring:** Spyware secretly monitors user activity, collecting sensitive information without the user's knowledge or consent. This is correctly matched.

3. **Ransomware and file encryption:** Ransomware encrypts the victim's files, making them inaccessible until a ransom is paid. This is correctly matched.

4. **Virus and rapid spread:** While viruses don't always spread rapidly, they do self-replicate, infecting other files or systems. This is a reasonable simplification and a correct match within the context of the question.


All four pairs accurately describe the method of operation for the given malware types.  Therefore, the correct answer is (d). The question evaluates the ability to differentiate various types of malware based on their functionalities.

**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Material                       Property
1. Graphene                     :   High melting point
2. Tantalum                      :   Excellent thermal conductivity
3.  Vanadium                     :  High corrosion resistance


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 3 only
(d) 1 and 3 only

**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Graphene, a single layer of carbon atoms arranged in a hexagonal lattice, is known for its exceptional thermal conductivity and electrical conductivity, not a high melting point.  Graphite, a form of carbon from which graphene is derived, has a very high melting point, but graphene itself does not exhibit the same characteristics in the same way.  Tantalum is indeed a rare metal with high corrosion resistance and a very high melting point, making it suitable for applications where extreme conditions are present. Vanadium, a transition metal, is also known for its high strength-to-weight ratio and its use in enhancing the tensile strength of steel, but its primary notable property isn't high corrosion resistance compared to tantalum which is renowned for its exceptional corrosion resistance, even at elevated temperatures. Therefore, only pair 2 is correctly matched.


**2. Consider the following pairs:**

   Technology                     Application
1.  Giant Magnetoresistance       :   Solar cells
2.  Brain-Computer Interface     :   Treatment of neurological disorders
3.  3D Printing                  :   Construction of hyperloop tunnels


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 2 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3

**Correct Answer:** (c)

**Explanation:**

Giant magnetoresistance (GMR) is a phenomenon where the electrical resistance of a material changes significantly in the presence of a magnetic field.  Its primary application is in data storage devices like hard disk drives, not in solar cells which utilize photovoltaic effects. Brain-computer interfaces (BCIs) are indeed being developed for potential applications in treating neurological disorders and enabling communication for individuals with paralysis.  3D printing, also known as additive manufacturing, is a versatile technology applicable across numerous sectors, including aerospace, construction and biomedical engineering. Its use in constructing hyperloop tunnels, considering the hyperloop's design, would be a potential and feasible application. Therefore, only pairs 2 and 3 are correctly matched.


**3. Consider the following pairs:**

   Element/Compound                 Feature/Use
1.  White Phosphorus                 :   Component in fertilizers
2.  Supercritical Carbon Dioxide     :    Enhanced oil recovery
3.  Tantalum                         :   Substitute for Platinum


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 2 only
(c) 2 and 3 only
(d) 1, 2 and 3

**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

White phosphorus, while also having military applications as an incendiary agent, is indeed a component in certain fertilizers. Supercritical carbon dioxide, a fluid state of CO2 beyond its critical point, shows promise in enhanced oil recovery techniques by flushing out oil from depleted reservoirs.  Tantalum, due to its high melting point and corrosion resistance, can serve as a substitute for platinum in certain applications where cost is a factor and high temperature resistance is needed.  Therefore, all three pairs are correctly matched.


**4. Consider the following pairs:**

   Isotope                           Application
1. Calcium-41                      :   Radiometric dating of organic materials older than 50,000 years
2. Carbon-14                      :   Radiometric dating of relatively recent organic materials
3.  Potassium-40/Argon-40         :  Radiometric dating of rocks


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 2 only

**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Calcium-41, while a long-lived radioisotope used in radiometric dating through a technique called Atom-Trap Trace Analysis (ATTA), is not suitable for dating materials older than 50,000 years.  Carbon-14, with a half-life of 5,700 years, is effectively used for dating relatively recent organic materials.  Potassium-40/Argon-40 dating is a well-established method for determining the age of rocks and other geological materials. Thus, only pairs 2 and 3 are correctly matched.


**5. Consider the following pairs:**

   Material                         Type
1.  Lab-grown Diamonds            :  Produced from coke and pith
2.  Synthetic Graphite             :  Artificially manufactured
3.  Natural Graphite                :  High crystalline, Amorphous and Flake


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 2 only

**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Lab-grown diamonds are indeed artificially manufactured, but they are not produced from coke and pith. That process is associated with synthetic graphite production. Synthetic graphite is, correctly, artificially manufactured.  Natural graphite exists in various forms, including high crystalline, amorphous, and flake varieties.  Therefore, only pairs 2 and 3 are correctly matched.


**6. Consider the following pairs:**

  Concept/Technology              Description
1.  Meissner Effect               :   Expulsion of a magnetic field from a superconductor at room temperature
2.  Room-Temperature Superconductor :  Exhibits superconductivity at temperatures above 0C
3.  Cooper Pairs                   :   Loosely bound pairs of electrons formed at very low temperatures


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 and 3 only
(c) 1 and 3 only
(d) 2 only

**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

The Meissner effect is the expulsion of a magnetic field from a superconductor as it transitions to a superconducting state upon cooling below its critical temperature (Tc),  not at room temperature. Room-temperature superconductors, a highly sought-after material, would indeed exhibit superconductivity at temperatures above 0C. Cooper pairs are the loosely bound electron pairs responsible for superconductivity, formed when temperatures are lowered below a critical level, enabling unimpeded electron flow.  Therefore, pairs 2 and 3 are correctly matched.

   Type of Robot                  Example
1. Industrial Robot                 :   Surgical robot

3. Medical Robot                   :   Robot used in manufacturing


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 2 and 3 only
(d) None

**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Industrial robots are primarily used in manufacturing processes, not in surgical procedures.  Service robots perform tasks in various non-manufacturing settings; a delivery drone is a good example. Medical robots are specifically designed for healthcare applications, such as surgery. Therefore, only pair 2 is correctly matched.  The other options incorrectly associate robot types with their applications.


**8. Consider the following pairs:**

   Nanomaterial                    Characteristic
1. Gold Nanoparticles              :   Photoacoustic properties

3. Hybrid Nanoparticles (Gold and Copper Sulphide) : Size less than 8nm


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 2 only
(c) 1 and 2 only
(d) 1, 2, and 3

**Correct Answer:** (d)

**Explanation:**

Gold nanoparticles can indeed exhibit photoacoustic properties, meaning they absorb light and generate ultrasound waves, useful in diagnostics. Copper sulphide nanoparticles possess photothermal properties, generating heat when exposed to light, a characteristic useful in cancer treatment.  Hybrid nanoparticles, combining gold and copper sulphide, are often less than 8nm in size.  Therefore, all three pairs are correctly matched.  The combination of properties makes them suitable for combined diagnostic and therapeutic applications.

**1. Consider the following pairs:**

   Technology/Technique                      Application/Use
1.  CRISPR-Cas9 gene editing              :   Producing low-pungent mustard varieties
2.  Aerial metagenomics                    :   Analyzing soil microbial communities
3.  Wolbachia method                         :   Controlling the spread of malaria
4.  Microsatellite DNA analysis            :   Studying genetic diversity in plant populations
5.  Genetic engineering of crops           :   Increasing phosphorus content in crops


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 only
(b) 1 and 4 only
(c) 1, 3 and 5 only
(d) 1, 2, 4, and 5


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

CRISPR-Cas9 is a precise gene-editing tool used to modify specific genes within an organism's genome.  Its application in developing low-pungent mustard varieties by altering genes responsible for glucosinolate production is a well-documented example.  Microsatellite DNA analysis, which focuses on short, repetitive DNA sequences, is a powerful tool for studying genetic variation within and between populations of organisms, including plants.  Therefore, pairs 1 and 4 are correctly matched.

Option (a) is incorrect because while CRISPR-Cas9 is correctly matched, the other pairs are not.  Option (c) is incorrect as the Wolbachia method is primarily used for controlling mosquito-borne diseases, not malaria specifically. While genetic engineering can indirectly affect nutrient content, directly increasing phosphorus is not its primary aim.  Option (d) is incorrect because aerial metagenomics is used to analyze airborne microbial communities, not soil communities.  The technique's focus is on the genetic material in the air, not soil samples.


**2. Consider the following pairs:**

   Disease                                     Vector/Agent
1.  Dengue fever                             :   Aedes aegypti mosquito
2.  Zika fever                               :   Culex mosquito
3.  Chikungunya                              :   Aedes albopictus mosquito
4.  Malaria                                  :   Anopheles mosquito


Which of the pairs given above is/are correctly matched?
(a) 1 and 3 only
(b) 1, 3, and 4 only
(c) 2 and 4 only
(d) 1, 2, 3, and 4


**Correct Answer:** (b)

**Explanation:**

Dengue fever and chikungunya are both arboviruses transmitted primarily by Aedes aegypti and Aedes albopictus mosquitoes, respectively.  Malaria is caused by Plasmodium parasites and transmitted by Anopheles mosquitoes.  Therefore, pairs 1, 3, and 4 are correctly matched.

Option (a) is incorrect because it omits the correct pairing of malaria and Anopheles mosquitoes. Option (c) is incorrect because it wrongly pairs Zika virus with the Culex mosquito. While Culex mosquitoes can transmit some viruses, Zika is primarily spread by Aedes mosquitoes. Option (d) is incorrect because it includes the incorrect pairing of Zika fever and Culex mosquitoes.

   Biotechnology Technique                 Specific Application

Plant tissue culture techniques, including embryo culture, seed culture, and organ culture, are widely used in plant biotechnology. Seed culture enables mass propagation of valuable plants. Organ culture allows scientists to study the effects of plant hormones and other factors on specific plant parts. Therefore, all four pairs are correctly matched.  All options except (d) are incorrect because they exclude at least one correctly matched pair.

**5. With reference to the applications of Artificial Intelligence (AI) in agriculture, consider the following pairs:**

     AI Application                           Specific Agricultural Use
